`src/module.rs`:

```rs
use std::rc::Rc;

use vmi::{
    Va, VmiError, VmiRead,
    os::{
        VmiOsModule as _, VmiOsUserModule as _,
        windows::{ArchAdapter, WindowsModule, WindowsUserModule},
    },
};

#[derive(Debug)]
struct ModuleRef {
    name: String,
    base_address: Va,
    size: u32,
    time_date_stamp: u32,
}

impl<Driver> TryFrom<WindowsModule<'_, Driver>> for ModuleRef
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    type Error = VmiError;

    fn try_from(value: WindowsModule<Driver>) -> Result<Self, Self::Error> {
        let name = match value.name() {
            Ok(name) => name,
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to read _KLDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.BaseDllName");
                return Err(err);
            }
        };

        let base_address = match value.base_address() {
            Ok(base_address) => base_address,
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to read _KLDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.DllBase");
                return Err(err);
            }
        };

        let size = match value.size() {
            Ok(size) => size as u32,
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to read _KLDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.SizeOfImage");
                return Err(err);
            }
        };

        let time_date_stamp = match value.time_date_stamp() {
            Ok(time_date_stamp) => time_date_stamp,
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to read _KLDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.TimeDateStamp");
                return Err(err);
            }
        };

        Ok(Self {
            name,
            base_address,
            size,
            time_date_stamp,
        })
    }
}

impl<Driver> TryFrom<WindowsUserModule<'_, Driver>> for ModuleRef
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    type Error = VmiError;

    fn try_from(value: WindowsUserModule<Driver>) -> Result<Self, Self::Error> {
        let name = match value.name() {
            Ok(name) => name,
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to read _LDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.BaseDllName");
                return Err(err);
            }
        };

        let base_address = match value.base_address() {
            Ok(base_address) => base_address,
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to read _LDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.DllBase");
                return Err(err);
            }
        };

        let size = match value.size() {
            Ok(size) => size as u32,
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to read _LDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.SizeOfImage");
                return Err(err);
            }
        };

        let time_date_stamp = match value.time_date_stamp() {
            Ok(time_date_stamp) => time_date_stamp,
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to read _LDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.TimeDateStamp");
                return Err(err);
            }
        };

        Ok(Self {
            name,
            base_address,
            size,
            time_date_stamp,
        })
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ModuleEntry {
    inner: Rc<ModuleRef>,
}

impl ModuleEntry {
    fn new(inner: ModuleRef) -> Self {
        Self {
            inner: Rc::new(inner),
        }
    }

    /// Corresponds to `_(K)LDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.BaseDllName`.
    pub fn name(&self) -> &str {
        &self.inner.name
    }

    /// Corresponds to `_(K)LDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.DllBase`.
    pub fn base_address(&self) -> Va {
        self.inner.base_address
    }

    /// Corresponds to `_(K)LDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.SizeOfImage`.
    pub fn size(&self) -> u32 {
        self.inner.size
    }

    /// Corresponds to `_(K)LDR_DATA_TABLE_ENTRY.TimeDateStamp`.
    pub fn time_date_stamp(&self) -> u32 {
        self.inner.time_date_stamp
    }
}

impl<Driver> TryFrom<WindowsModule<'_, Driver>> for ModuleEntry
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    type Error = VmiError;

    fn try_from(value: WindowsModule<Driver>) -> Result<Self, Self::Error> {
        Ok(Self::new(ModuleRef::try_from(value)?))
    }
}

impl<Driver> TryFrom<WindowsUserModule<'_, Driver>> for ModuleEntry
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    type Error = VmiError;

    fn try_from(value: WindowsUserModule<Driver>) -> Result<Self, Self::Error> {
        Ok(Self::new(ModuleRef::try_from(value)?))
    }
}

```

`src/process.rs`:

```rs
use std::{
    cell::{Ref, RefCell},
    collections::{BTreeMap, HashMap},
    rc::Rc,
};

use vmi::{
    Pa, Va, VmiError, VmiRead, VmiState,
    os::{
        ProcessObject, VmiOsProcess,
        windows::{ArchAdapter, WindowsOs},
    },
};

use super::module::ModuleEntry;

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
pub enum ProcessEntryKind {
    System,
    User,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
struct ProcessRef {
    kind: ProcessEntryKind,
    name: String,
    process_object: ProcessObject,
    translation_root: Pa,
    modules: BTreeMap<Va, ModuleEntry>,
}

impl ProcessRef {
    pub fn new<Driver>(
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        process_object: ProcessObject,
        flags: ProcessPreloadFlags,
    ) -> Result<Self, VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        let process = vmi.os().process(process_object)?;
        let name = process.name()?;
        let translation_root = process.translation_root()?;

        let kind = if process_object == vmi.os().system_process()?.object()? {
            ProcessEntryKind::System
        }
        else {
            ProcessEntryKind::User
        };

        let modules = match kind {
            ProcessEntryKind::System
                if flags.contains(ProcessPreloadFlags::PRELOAD_SYSTEM_MODULES) =>
            {
                collect_modules(vmi, kind, process_object)?
            }
            ProcessEntryKind::User if flags.contains(ProcessPreloadFlags::PRELOAD_USER_MODULES) => {
                collect_modules(vmi, kind, process_object)?
            }
            _ => BTreeMap::new(),
        };

        Ok(Self {
            kind,
            name,
            process_object,
            translation_root,
            modules,
        })
    }

    pub fn name(&self) -> &str {
        &self.name
    }

    pub fn process_object(&self) -> ProcessObject {
        self.process_object
    }

    pub fn translation_root(&self) -> Pa {
        self.translation_root
    }

    pub fn lookup_module(&self, va: Va) -> Option<ModuleEntry> {
        let (_, module) = self.modules.range(..=va).next_back()?;

        if va >= module.base_address() + module.size() as u64 {
            return None;
        }

        Some(module.clone())
    }

    pub fn lookup_or_insert_module<Driver>(
        &mut self,
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        va: Va,
    ) -> Result<Option<ModuleEntry>, VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        if let Some(module) = self.lookup_module(va) {
            return Ok(Some(module));
        }

        self.lookup_and_insert_module(vmi, va)
    }

    pub fn preload_modules<Driver>(
        &mut self,
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
    ) -> Result<(), VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        self.modules = collect_modules(vmi, self.kind, self.process_object)?;
        Ok(())
    }

    fn lookup_and_insert_module<Driver>(
        &mut self,
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        va: Va,
    ) -> Result<Option<ModuleEntry>, VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        let module = match self.kind {
            ProcessEntryKind::System => {
                iter_system_modules(vmi)?.find(|module| contains(module, va))
            }
            ProcessEntryKind::User => {
                iter_user_modules(vmi, self.process_object)?.find(|module| contains(module, va))
            }
        };

        let module = match module {
            Some(module) => module,
            None => return Ok(None),
        };

        self.modules.insert(module.base_address(), module);

        Ok(self.lookup_module(va))
    }
}

fn contains(module: &ModuleEntry, va: Va) -> bool {
    va >= module.base_address() && va < module.base_address() + module.size() as u64
}

fn collect_modules<Driver>(
    vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
    kind: ProcessEntryKind,
    process_object: ProcessObject,
) -> Result<BTreeMap<Va, ModuleEntry>, VmiError>
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    let mut modules = BTreeMap::new();

    match kind {
        ProcessEntryKind::System => {
            for module in iter_system_modules(vmi)? {
                modules.insert(module.base_address(), module);
            }
        }
        ProcessEntryKind::User => {
            for module in iter_user_modules(vmi, process_object)? {
                modules.insert(module.base_address(), module);
            }
        }
    }

    Ok(modules)
}

fn iter_system_modules<Driver>(
    vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
) -> Result<impl Iterator<Item = ModuleEntry>, VmiError>
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    Ok(vmi.os().modules()?.flat_map(|module| {
        module
            .and_then(ModuleEntry::try_from)
            .inspect_err(|err| tracing::warn!(%err, "failed to read module, skipping"))
            .ok()
    }))
}

fn iter_user_modules<Driver>(
    vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
    process_object: ProcessObject,
) -> Result<impl Iterator<Item = ModuleEntry>, VmiError>
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    Ok(
        vmi.os().process(process_object)?
            .peb().inspect_err(|err| tracing::warn!(%err, "failed to read _PEB"))
            .ok().flatten()
            .and_then(|peb| {
                peb.ldr()
                    .inspect_err(|err| tracing::warn!(%err, "failed to read _PEB.Ldr"))
                    .ok()
            })
            .and_then(|ldr| {
                ldr.in_load_order_modules()
                    .inspect_err(|err| tracing::warn!(%err, "failed to read _PEB_LDR_DATA.InLoadOrderModuleList"))
                    .ok()
            })
            .into_iter().flatten()
            .filter_map(|module| {
                module
                    .and_then(ModuleEntry::try_from)
                    .inspect_err(|err| tracing::warn!(%err, "failed to read module, skipping"))
                    .ok()
            })
    )
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ProcessEntry {
    inner: Rc<RefCell<ProcessRef>>,
}

impl ProcessEntry {
    pub fn new<Driver>(
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        process_object: ProcessObject,
        flags: ProcessPreloadFlags,
    ) -> Result<Self, VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        Ok(Self {
            inner: Rc::new(RefCell::new(ProcessRef::new(vmi, process_object, flags)?)),
        })
    }

    pub fn name(&self) -> Ref<'_, str> {
        Ref::map(self.inner.borrow(), |inner| inner.name())
    }

    pub fn process_object(&self) -> ProcessObject {
        self.inner.borrow().process_object()
    }

    pub fn translation_root(&self) -> Pa {
        self.inner.borrow().translation_root()
    }

    pub fn preload_modules<Driver>(
        &self,
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
    ) -> Result<(), VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        self.inner.borrow_mut().preload_modules(vmi)
    }

    pub fn lookup_module<Driver>(
        &self,
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        va: Va,
    ) -> Result<Option<ModuleEntry>, VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        self.inner.borrow_mut().lookup_or_insert_module(vmi, va)
    }
}

bitflags::bitflags! {
    #[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq)]
    pub struct ProcessPreloadFlags: u32 {
        const PRELOAD_SYSTEM_MODULES = 0x1;
        const PRELOAD_USER_MODULES = 0x2;
    }
}

pub struct ProcessManager {
    processes: HashMap<ProcessObject, ProcessEntry>,
    system_process_object: ProcessObject,
}

impl ProcessManager {
    pub fn new<Driver>(
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        flags: ProcessPreloadFlags,
    ) -> Result<Self, VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        let mut processes = HashMap::new();
        let system_process_object = vmi.os().system_process()?.object()?;

        for process in vmi.os().processes()? {
            let process = match process {
                Ok(process) => process,
                Err(err) => {
                    tracing::warn!(%err, "failed to read PsActiveProcessHead entry");
                    continue;
                }
            };

            let process_object = process.object()?;

            let entry = ProcessEntry::new(vmi, process_object, flags)?;
            processes.insert(process_object, entry);
        }

        Ok(Self {
            processes,
            system_process_object,
        })
    }

    pub fn iter(&self) -> impl Iterator<Item = ProcessEntry> {
        self.processes.values().cloned()
    }

    pub fn get(&self, process_object: ProcessObject) -> Option<ProcessEntry> {
        self.processes.get(&process_object).cloned()
    }

    pub fn system_process_object(&self) -> ProcessObject {
        self.system_process_object
    }

    fn target_process_object(&self, process_object: ProcessObject, va: Va) -> ProcessObject {
        if (va.0 as i64) < 0 {
            self.system_process_object
        }
        else {
            process_object
        }
    }

    pub fn lookup_module<Driver>(
        &self,
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        process_object: ProcessObject,
        va: Va,
    ) -> Result<Option<ModuleEntry>, VmiError>
    where
        Driver: VmiRead,
        Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
    {
        let target_process_object = self.target_process_object(process_object, va);

        let entry = match self.processes.get(&target_process_object) {
            Some(entry) => entry,
            None => return Ok(None),
        };

        entry.lookup_module(vmi, va)
    }
}
```

`src/resolver.rs`:

```rs
//! Session management for crash dump analysis.
//!
//! Wraps the VMI session with module enumeration and symbol resolution
//! support, providing the core state needed by all commands.

use std::{collections::HashMap, fs::File, rc::Rc};

use isr::{
    Profile,
    cache::{CodeView, Entry, IsrCache},
    download::windows::ImageSignature,
};
use memmap2::Mmap;
use vmi::{
    Va, VmiError, VmiRead, VmiState,
    os::windows::{
        ArchAdapter, PeFile, PeImage, WindowsOs, unwind::amd64::resolve_primary_function,
    },
};

use super::module::ModuleEntry;

self_cell::self_cell! {
    /// A cached PE binary: owns the memory-mapped file data and a parsed
    /// [`PeFile`] that borrows from it.
    struct ImageRef {
        owner: Mmap,
        #[covariant]
        dependent: PeFile,
    }
}

#[derive(Clone)]
pub struct ImageEntry {
    inner: Rc<ImageRef>,
}

impl ImageEntry {
    pub fn pe_file(&self) -> &PeFile<'_> {
        self.inner.borrow_dependent()
    }
}

self_cell::self_cell! {
    /// A symbol profile owning its memory-mapped data.
    ///
    /// The [`Profile`] borrows symbol names directly from the mmap'd
    /// profile data, avoiding per-symbol String allocations.
    struct ProfileEntry {
        owner: Entry,
        #[covariant]
        dependent: Profile,
    }
}

#[derive(thiserror::Error, Debug)]
pub enum ResolverError {
    #[error(transparent)]
    Io(#[from] std::io::Error),

    #[error("ISR cache error: {0}")]
    IsrCache(#[from] isr::cache::Error),

    #[error("ISR decode error: {0}")]
    IsrDecode(Box<dyn std::error::Error + Send + Sync>),

    #[error("PE error: {0}")]
    Pe(#[from] vmi::os::windows::pe::PeError),

    #[error("VMI error: {0}")]
    Vmi(#[from] VmiError),
}

/// A resolved symbol with module name, function name, and offset.
pub struct ResolvedSymbol {
    /// Display name of the module (e.g. "nt" for ntoskrnl.exe).
    pub module_name: String,
    /// Function name from the PDB, or empty if unknown.
    pub function_name: String,
    /// Offset from the start of the function (or from module base if no symbol).
    pub offset: u64,
}

/// Analysis session holding VMI state, ISR cache, kernel modules, and
/// per-process state.
pub struct Resolver<Driver>
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    /// ISR cache for downloading PDBs and PE binaries.
    isr: IsrCache,

    /// Cached PE binaries, keyed by module base address.
    /// `None` means the PE failed to download/parse (prevents retrying).
    image_cache: HashMap<Va, Option<ImageEntry>>,

    /// Cached symbol profiles, keyed by module name.
    /// `None` means the profile failed to load (prevents retrying).
    profile_cache: HashMap<String, Option<ProfileEntry>>,

    _marker: std::marker::PhantomData<Driver>,
}

impl<Driver> Resolver<Driver>
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    /// Creates a new resolver with the given ISR cache.
    pub fn new(isr: IsrCache) -> Self {
        Self {
            isr,
            image_cache: HashMap::new(),
            profile_cache: HashMap::new(),
            _marker: std::marker::PhantomData,
        }
    }

    /// Returns the cached PE binary for the given module, downloading
    /// it from the symbol server if needed.
    pub fn resolve_image(&mut self, module: &ModuleEntry) -> Option<ImageEntry> {
        // Return existing entry (or cached failure) if present.
        if let Some(entry) = self.image_cache.get(&module.base_address()) {
            return entry.clone();
        }

        match self.load_image(module) {
            Ok(image) => {
                self.image_cache
                    .insert(module.base_address(), Some(image.clone()));
                Some(image)
            }
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, module = module.name(), "failed to load PE image");
                self.image_cache.insert(module.base_address(), None);
                None
            }
        }
    }

    fn load_image(&self, module: &ModuleEntry) -> Result<ImageEntry, ResolverError> {
        let image_signature = ImageSignature {
            name: module.name().to_owned(),
            timestamp: module.time_date_stamp(),
            size_of_image: module.size(),
        };

        let binary_path = self.isr.download_from_image_signature(image_signature)?;
        let mmap = File::open(&binary_path).and_then(|file| unsafe { Mmap::map(&file) })?;
        Ok(ImageEntry {
            inner: Rc::new(ImageRef::try_new(mmap, |data| {
                PeFile::new(data).map_err(ResolverError::Pe)
            })?),
        })
    }

    /// Resolves a virtual address to a symbol within the given module.
    ///
    /// Uses the PE exception directory (.pdata) to follow
    /// `UNW_FLAG_CHAININFO` chains, resolving function chunks back to
    /// their primary function before looking up the PDB symbol.
    ///
    /// Lazily loads PDB symbols for the module on first access.
    /// Falls back to module+offset if the PDB cannot be loaded.
    pub fn resolve_symbol(
        &mut self,
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        module: &ModuleEntry,
        va: Va,
    ) -> ResolvedSymbol {
        let rva = va.0.saturating_sub(module.base_address().0);

        // Resolve function chunks to the primary function via .pdata
        // chain following. This handles MSVC-split functions where code
        // chunks are scattered across the binary.
        let primary_rva = self
            .resolve_image(module)
            .and_then(|image| resolve_primary_function(image.pe_file(), rva as u32).ok()?)
            .map(|rva| rva as u64)
            .unwrap_or(rva);

        // Ensure symbols are loaded (or marked as failed) for this module.
        if !self.profile_cache.contains_key(module.name()) {
            self.load_symbols(vmi, module);
        }

        // Look up the symbol using the primary function RVA.
        // The offset is from the primary function start, not the chunk start.
        if let Some(Some(profile)) = self.profile_cache.get(module.name())
            && let Some(entry) = profile.borrow_dependent().lookup_symbol(primary_rva)
        {
            return ResolvedSymbol {
                module_name: module.name().to_string(),
                function_name: entry.name.to_string(),
                offset: rva - entry.rva,
            };
        }

        // Fallback: no matching symbol found.
        ResolvedSymbol {
            module_name: module.name().to_string(),
            function_name: String::new(),
            offset: rva,
        }
    }

    /// Loads PDB symbols for a module.
    fn load_symbols(&mut self, vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>, module: &ModuleEntry) {
        match self.try_load_symbols(vmi, module) {
            Ok(Some(profile)) => {
                tracing::debug!(
                    module = module.name(),
                    symbols = profile.borrow_dependent().symbols().len(),
                    "loaded symbols"
                );
                self.profile_cache
                    .insert(module.name().to_string(), Some(profile));
            }
            Ok(None) => {
                tracing::debug!(module = module.name(), "no symbols found");
                self.profile_cache.insert(module.name().to_string(), None);
            }
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, module = module.name(), "failed to load symbols");
                self.profile_cache.insert(module.name().to_string(), None);
            }
        }
    }

    /// Attempts to load PDB symbols for a module.
    fn try_load_symbols(
        &mut self,
        vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
        module: &ModuleEntry,
    ) -> Result<Option<ProfileEntry>, ResolverError> {
        let image = vmi.os().image(module.base_address())?;

        match self.load_from_image(&image) {
            Ok(Some(profile)) => Ok(Some(profile)),
            Ok(None) => Ok(None),
            Err(err) => {
                tracing::debug!(%err, "failed to load symbols from PE image, trying cached PE file");
                let image_entry = match self.resolve_image(module) {
                    Some(entry) => entry,
                    None => return Ok(None),
                };

                self.load_from_image(image_entry.pe_file())
            }
        }
    }

    fn load_from_image(
        &mut self,
        image: &impl PeImage,
    ) -> Result<Option<ProfileEntry>, ResolverError> {
        let debug_directory = match image.debug_directory()? {
            Some(debug_directory) => debug_directory,
            None => return Ok(None),
        };

        let codeview = match debug_directory.codeview()? {
            Some(codeview) => codeview,
            None => return Ok(None),
        };

        Ok(Some(self.load_from_codeview(codeview)?))
    }

    /// Loads symbols from a CodeView reference.
    fn load_from_codeview(&self, codeview: CodeView) -> Result<ProfileEntry, ResolverError> {
        let entry = self.isr.entry_from_codeview(codeview)?;

        ProfileEntry::try_new(entry, |entry| unsafe { entry.profile_unchecked() })
            .map_err(|err| ResolverError::IsrDecode(Box::new(err)))
    }
}
```

`src/walkstack.rs`:

```rs
//! Stack backtrace command (`kb`).
//!
//! Walks the call stack using PE unwind information and prints
//! WinDbg-compatible output with resolved symbols. Handles the
//! kernel/user-mode boundary via machine frame detection.

use vmi::{
    Va, VmiError, VmiRead, VmiState,
    os::{
        ProcessObject, ThreadObject,
        windows::{
            ArchAdapter, WindowsOs,
            unwind::{
                Frame, Unwinder as _, Unwound,
                amd64::{UnwindContextAmd64, UnwinderAmd64, read_params, unwind_leaf},
            },
        },
    },
};

use super::{Ephemera, module::ModuleEntry};

/// Result of building an unwind context.
#[derive(Clone)]
pub struct UnwindTarget {
    /// The process whose address space to use.
    pub process_object: ProcessObject,
    /// The thread being unwound.
    pub thread_object: ThreadObject,
    /// Initial register state.
    pub context: UnwindContextAmd64,
}

/// A stack frame paired with its call site address.
///
/// The raw unwinder's [`Frame::instruction_pointer`] is the return
/// address (caller's IP). `call_site` is the IP of the function that
/// made the call - what WinDbg shows in the "Call Site" column.
pub struct WalkFrame {
    /// This frame's instruction pointer (the function being executed).
    pub call_site: Va,

    /// Stack pointer at the start of this frame, before unwinding it.
    /// Matches WinDbg's `Child-SP` column and the `TrapFrame @ <addr>`
    /// address emitted by `kv` for trap-handler frames.
    pub child_sp: Va,

    /// The raw unwinder frame (`instruction_pointer` = return address).
    pub frame: Frame,
}

/// Walks the call stack, yielding one [`WalkFrame`] per iteration.
///
/// Each yielded frame includes the call site IP and the raw unwind
/// result. The final bottom-of-stack frame (return address zero) is
/// included.
pub fn walk_stack<Driver>(
    vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
    session: &Ephemera<Driver>,
    mut target: UnwindTarget,
) -> impl Iterator<Item = Result<WalkFrame, VmiError>>
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    let unwinder = UnwinderAmd64;
    let mut done = false;

    std::iter::from_fn(move || {
        if done {
            return None;
        }

        let call_site = Va(target.context.rip);
        let child_sp = Va(target.context.rsp);

        match unwind(vmi, session, &unwinder, &mut target) {
            Ok(Unwound::Frame(frame)) => Some(Ok(WalkFrame {
                call_site,
                child_sp,
                frame,
            })),
            Ok(end) => {
                done = true;

                let machine_frame = matches!(end, Unwound::MachineEnd);
                let stack_pointer = Va(target.context.rsp);
                let params = read_params(&vmi, stack_pointer);

                Some(Ok(WalkFrame {
                    call_site,
                    child_sp,
                    frame: Frame {
                        instruction_pointer: Va(0),
                        stack_pointer,
                        params,
                        machine_frame,
                    },
                }))
            }
            Err(_) => {
                done = true;

                let stack_pointer = Va(target.context.rsp);
                let params = read_params(&vmi, stack_pointer);

                Some(Ok(WalkFrame {
                    call_site,
                    child_sp,
                    frame: Frame {
                        instruction_pointer: Va(0),
                        stack_pointer,
                        params,
                        machine_frame: false,
                    },
                }))
            }
        }
    })
}

fn unwind<Driver>(
    vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
    session: &Ephemera<Driver>,
    unwinder: &UnwinderAmd64,
    target: &mut UnwindTarget,
) -> Result<Unwound, VmiError>
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    match session.lookup_module(vmi, target.process_object, Va(target.context.rip))? {
        Some(module) => unwind_with_fallback(vmi, session, unwinder, &module, &mut target.context),
        None => unwind_leaf(&vmi, &mut target.context),
    }
}

/// Attempts to unwind one frame using the VMI image, falling back to
/// a downloaded PE binary if the .pdata pages are not in the dump.
fn unwind_with_fallback<Driver>(
    vmi: VmiState<'_, WindowsOs<Driver>>,
    session: &Ephemera<Driver>,
    unwinder: &UnwinderAmd64,
    module: &ModuleEntry,
    context: &mut UnwindContextAmd64,
) -> Result<Unwound, VmiError>
where
    Driver: VmiRead,
    Driver::Architecture: ArchAdapter<Driver>,
{
    let image = vmi.os().image(module.base_address())?;
    match unwinder.unwind(&vmi, module.base_address(), &image, context) {
        Ok(result) => Ok(result),
        Err(err) => {
            tracing::debug!(%err, "VMI unwind failed, trying PE file unwind");
            let image = match session.resolve_image(module) {
                Some(image) => image,
                None => {
                    tracing::debug!("no PE file found for module, cannot unwind");
                    return Ok(Unwound::End);
                }
            };

            unwinder.unwind(&vmi, module.base_address(), image.pe_file(), context)
        }
    }
}
```
